#Create a simulator object
set ns [new Simulator]

#Define different colors for data flows (for NAM)
$ns color 1 Red
$ns color 2 Blue
$ns color 3 Green
$ns color 4 Yellow
$ns color 5 Black

#Open the NAM trace file
set nf [open /home/lucas/Documents/ns2/nsOutput/normalupload100_scriptNS2_7638544921.nam w]
$ns namtrace-all $nf

#Define a 'finish' procedure
proc finish {} {
	global ns nf
	$ns flush-trace
	#Close the NAM trace file
	close $nf
	exit 0
}

#Server Moodle
set internet [$ns node]
set server [$ns node]
$ns duplex-link $internet $server 100Mb 60ms DropTail

#Create nodes Polo 1
set S1 [$ns node]
$ns simplex-link $internet $S1 20Mb 50ms DropTail
$ns simplex-link $S1 $internet 20Mb 50ms DropTail

#Create connection TCP Polo 1


#Polo 1 Maquina 1 -- Servidor
set tcpP1M1ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP1M1ToServer set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $P1M1 $tcpP1M1ToServer
set sinkP1M1ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP1M1ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP1M1ToServer $sinkP1M1ToServer
$tcpP1M1ToServer set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP1M1ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP1M1ToServer attach-agent $tcpP1M1ToServer
$ftpP1M1ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 1 Maquina 1
set tcpServerToP1M1 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP1M1 set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP1M1
set sinkServerToP1M1 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P1M1 $sinkServerToP1M1
$ns connect $tcpServerToP1M1 $sinkServerToP1M1
$tcpServerToP1M1 set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP1M1 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP1M1 attach-agent $tcpServerToP1M1
$ftpServerToP1M1 set type_ FTP

#Polo 1 Maquina 2 -- Servidor

$ns connect $tcpP1M25ToServer $sinkP1M25ToServer
$tcpP1M25ToServer set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP1M25ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP1M25ToServer attach-agent $tcpP1M25ToServer
$ftpP1M25ToServer set type_ FTP

$tcpP3M15ToServer set class_ 3
$ns attach-agent $P3M15 $tcpP3M15ToServer
set sinkP3M15ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP3M15ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP3M15ToServer $sinkP3M15ToServer
$tcpP3M15ToServer set fid_ 3
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP3M15ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP3M15ToServer attach-agent $tcpP3M15ToServer
$ftpP3M15ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 3 Maquina 15
set tcpServerToP3M15 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP3M15 set class_ 3
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP3M15
set sinkServerToP3M15 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P3M15 $sinkServerToP3M15
$ns connect $tcpServerToP3M15 $sinkServerToP3M15
$tcpServerToP3M15 set fid_ 3
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP3M15 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP3M15 attach-agent $tcpServerToP3M15
$ftpServerToP3M15 set type_ FTP

$ftpServerToP4M7 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M7
$ftpServerToP4M7 set type_ FTP

#Polo 4 Maquina 8 -- Servidor
set tcpP4M8ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP4M8ToServer set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $P4M8 $tcpP4M8ToServer
set sinkP4M8ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP4M8ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP4M8ToServer $sinkP4M8ToServer
$tcpP4M8ToServer set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP4M8ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP4M8ToServer attach-agent $tcpP4M8ToServer
$ftpP4M8ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 4 Maquina 8
set tcpServerToP4M8 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP4M8 set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP4M8
set sinkServerToP4M8 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P4M8 $sinkServerToP4M8
$ns connect $tcpServerToP4M8 $sinkServerToP4M8
$tcpServerToP4M8 set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP4M8 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP4M8 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M8
$ftpServerToP4M8 set type_ FTP

$ns connect $tcpServerToP4M47 $sinkServerToP4M47
$tcpServerToP4M47 set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP4M47 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP4M47 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M47
$ftpServerToP4M47 set type_ FTP
